<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-105">Cet article fournit des informations sur les erreurs de démarrage d’applications courantes et des instructions sur la façon de diagnostiquer les erreurs lorsqu’une application est déployée sur Azure App Service ou IIS :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-105">This article provides information on common app startup errors and instructions on how to diagnose errors when an app is deployed to Azure App Service or IIS:</span></span>

[<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-110">Résoudre les problèmes sur IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-110">Troubleshoot on IIS</span></span>](#troubleshoot-on-iis)  
<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-111">Fournit des conseils de dépannage pour les applications déployées à l’IIS ou en cours d’exécution sur IIS Express localement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-111">Provides troubleshooting advice for apps deployed to IIS or running on IIS Express locally.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-112">Les directives s’appliquent à la fois aux déploiements de bureau Windows Server et Windows.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-112">The guidance applies to both Windows Server and Windows desktop deployments.</span></span>

## <a name="app-startup-errors"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-117">Erreurs de démarrage des applications</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-117">App startup errors</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-118">Dans Visual Studio, un projet ASP.NET Core est par défaut hébergé sur [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview) pendant une opération de débogage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-118">In Visual Studio, an ASP.NET Core project defaults to [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview) hosting during debugging.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-119">Un *502.5 - Échec du processus* ou un *500.30 - Échec de démarrage* qui se produit lors de débogage localement peut être diagnostiqué en utilisant les conseils dans ce sujet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-119">A *502.5 - Process Failure* or a *500.30 - Start Failure* that occurs when debugging locally can be diagnosed using the advice in this topic.</span></span>

### <a name="40314-forbidden"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-120">403.14 Interdit</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-120">403.14 Forbidden</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-121">L’application ne démarre pas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-121">The app fails to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-122">L’erreur suivante est enregistrée :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-122">The following error is logged:</span></span>

```
The Web server is configured to not list the contents of this directory.
```

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-123">L’erreur est généralement causée par un déploiement interrompu sur le système d’hébergement, qui comprend l’un des scénarios suivants:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-123">The error is usually caused by a broken deployment on the hosting system, which includes any of the following scenarios:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-124">L’application est déployée dans le mauvais dossier sur le système d’hébergement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-124">The app is deployed to the wrong folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-125">Le processus de déploiement n’a pas permis de transférer tous les fichiers et dossiers de l’application dans le dossier de déploiement du système d’hébergement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-125">The deployment process failed to move all of the app's files and folders to the deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-126">Le fichier *web.config* est absent du déploiement, ou le contenu du fichier *web.config* sont malformés.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-126">The *web.config* file is missing from the deployment, or the *web.config* file contents are malformed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-127">Procédez comme suit :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-127">Perform the following steps:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-128">Supprimer tous les fichiers et dossiers du dossier de déploiement sur le système d’hébergement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-128">Delete all of the files and folders from the deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-129">Redéployez le contenu du dossier de *publication* de l’application sur le système d’hébergement en utilisant votre méthode normale de déploiement, comme Visual Studio, PowerShell ou déploiement manuel :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-129">Redeploy the contents of the app's *publish* folder to the hosting system using your normal method of deployment, such as Visual Studio, PowerShell, or manual deployment:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-130">Confirmez que le fichier *web.config* est présent dans le déploiement et que son contenu est correct.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-130">Confirm that the *web.config* file is present in the deployment and that its contents are correct.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-131">Lors de l’hébergement sur Azure App Service, confirmez que l’application est déployée dans le `D:\home\site\wwwroot` dossier.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-131">When hosting on Azure App Service, confirm that the app is deployed to the `D:\home\site\wwwroot` folder.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-132">Lorsque l’application est hébergée par l’IIS, confirmez que l’application est déployée sur le **chemin physique** de l’IIS indiqué dans **les paramètres**de base de **l’IIS Manager**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-132">When the app is hosted by IIS, confirm that the app is deployed to the IIS **Physical path** shown in **IIS Manager**'s **Basic Settings**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-133">Confirmez que tous les fichiers et dossiers de l’application sont déployés en comparant le déploiement sur le système d’hébergement au contenu du dossier de *publication* du projet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-133">Confirm that all of the app's files and folders are deployed by comparing the deployment on the hosting system to the contents of the project's *publish* folder.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-134">Pour plus d’informations sur la mise en page <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>d’une application ASP.NET Core publiée, voir .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-134">For more information on the layout of a published ASP.NET Core app, see <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-135">Pour plus d’informations sur le <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#configuration-with-webconfig>fichier *web.config,* voir .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-135">For more information on the *web.config* file, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#configuration-with-webconfig>.</span></span>

### <a name="500-internal-server-error"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-136">500 Erreur interne du serveur</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-136">500 Internal Server Error</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-137">L’application démarre, mais une erreur empêche le serveur de répondre à la requête.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-137">The app starts, but an error prevents the server from fulfilling the request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-138">Cette erreur se produit dans le code de l’application pendant le démarrage ou durant la création d’une réponse.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-138">This error occurs within the app's code during startup or while creating a response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-139">La réponse peut être dépourvue de contenu ou apparaître sous la forme d’une *erreur de serveur interne 500* dans le navigateur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-139">The response may contain no content, or the response may appear as a *500 Internal Server Error* in the browser.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-140">Le Journal des événements de l’application indique généralement qu’elle a démarré normalement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-140">The Application Event Log usually states that the app started normally.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-141">Du point de vue du serveur, c’est exact.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-141">From the server's perspective, that's correct.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-142">L’application a démarré, mais elle ne peut pas générer de réponse valide.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-142">The app did start, but it can't generate a valid response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-143">Exécutez l’application depuis une invite de commandes sur le serveur ou activez le journal stdout du module ASP.NET Core pour résoudre le problème.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-143">Run the app at a command prompt on the server or enable the ASP.NET Core Module stdout log to troubleshoot the problem.</span></span>

### <a name="5000-in-process-handler-load-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-144">500.0 - Échec de chargement du gestionnaire in-process</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-144">500.0 In-Process Handler Load Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-145">Le processus de travail échoue.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-145">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-146">L’application ne démarre pas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-146">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-147">Une erreur inconnue s’est produite en chargeant ASP.NET composants [du module de base.](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-147">An unknown error occurred loading [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) components.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-148">Effectuez l'une des opérations suivantes :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-148">Take one of the following actions:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-149">Contactez le [Support Microsoft](https://support.microsoft.com/oas/default.aspx?prid=15832) (sélectionnez **Outils de développement**, puis **ASP.NET Core**).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-149">Contact [Microsoft Support](https://support.microsoft.com/oas/default.aspx?prid=15832) (select **Developer Tools** then **ASP.NET Core**).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-150">Posez une question sur Stack Overflow.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-150">Ask a question on Stack Overflow.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-151">Signalez un problème sur notre [dépôt GitHub](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-151">File an issue on our [GitHub repository](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore).</span></span>

### <a name="50030-in-process-startup-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-152">500.30 - Échec du démarrage in-process</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-152">500.30 In-Process Startup Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-153">Le processus de travail échoue.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-153">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-154">L’application ne démarre pas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-154">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-155">Le [ASP.NET module de base](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) tente de démarrer le .NET Core CLR en cours de traitement, mais il ne démarre pas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-155">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) attempts to start the .NET Core CLR in-process, but it fails to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-156">Vous pouvez généralement déterminer la cause d’un échec de démarrage du processus à partir des entrées du Journal des événements de l’application et du journal stdout du module ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-156">The cause of a process startup failure can usually be determined from entries in the Application Event Log and the ASP.NET Core Module stdout log.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-157">Conditions d’échec communes :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-157">Common failure conditions:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-158">L’application est mal configurée en raison de cibler une version du cadre partagé ASP.NET Core qui n’est pas présent.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-158">The app is misconfigured due to targeting a version of the ASP.NET Core shared framework that isn't present.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-159">Vérifiez les versions du framework partagé ASP.NET Core qui sont installées sur l’ordinateur cible.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-159">Check which versions of the ASP.NET Core shared framework are installed on the target machine.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-160">Utilisation d’Azure Key Vault, manque d’autorisations pour le coffre-fort.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-160">Using Azure Key Vault, lack of permissions to the Key Vault.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-161">Vérifiez les stratégies d’accès dans le coffre-fort ciblé pour vous assurer que les autorisations correctes sont accordées.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-161">Check the access policies in the targeted Key Vault to ensure that the correct permissions are granted.</span></span>

### <a name="50031-ancm-failed-to-find-native-dependencies"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-162">500.31 - Échec de la recherche de dépendances natives par ANCM</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-162">500.31 ANCM Failed to Find Native Dependencies</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-163">Le processus de travail échoue.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-163">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-164">L’application ne démarre pas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-164">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-165">Le [ASP.NET module de base](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) tente de démarrer le processus d’exécution .NET Core, mais il ne démarre pas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-165">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) attempts to start the .NET Core runtime in-process, but it fails to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-166">La cause la plus courante de cet échec de démarrage est liée à la non-installation du runtime `Microsoft.NETCore.App` ou `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-166">The most common cause of this startup failure is when the `Microsoft.NETCore.App` or `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App` runtime isn't installed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-167">Si l’application est déployée pour cibler ASP.NET Core 3.0, et si cette version n’existe pas sur la machine, cette erreur se produit.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-167">If the app is deployed to target ASP.NET Core 3.0 and that version doesn't exist on the machine, this error occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-168">Voici un exemple de message d’erreur :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-168">An example error message follows:</span></span>

```
The specified framework 'Microsoft.NETCore.App', version '3.0.0' was not found.
  - The following frameworks were found:
      2.2.1 at [C:\Program Files\dotnet\x64\shared\Microsoft.NETCore.App]
      3.0.0-preview5-27626-15 at [C:\Program Files\dotnet\x64\shared\Microsoft.NETCore.App]
      3.0.0-preview6-27713-13 at [C:\Program Files\dotnet\x64\shared\Microsoft.NETCore.App]
      3.0.0-preview6-27714-15 at [C:\Program Files\dotnet\x64\shared\Microsoft.NETCore.App]
      3.0.0-preview6-27723-08 at [C:\Program Files\dotnet\x64\shared\Microsoft.NETCore.App]
```

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-169">Le message d’erreur liste toutes les versions installées de .NET Core ainsi que la version demandée par l’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-169">The error message lists all the installed .NET Core versions and the version requested by the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-170">Pour corriger cette erreur, vous avez le choix entre plusieurs possibilités :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-170">To fix this error, either:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-171">Installez la version appropriée de .NET Core sur la machine.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-171">Install the appropriate version of .NET Core on the machine.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-172">Changez l’application pour cibler une version de .NET Core présente sur la machine.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-172">Change the app to target a version of .NET Core that's present on the machine.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-173">Publiez l’application sous forme de [déploiement autonome](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-173">Publish the app as a [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-174">Durant l’exécution en phase de développement (la variable d’environnement `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` a la valeur `Development`), l’erreur spécifique est écrite dans la réponse HTTP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-174">When running in development (the `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` environment variable is set to `Development`), the specific error is written to the HTTP response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-175">La cause d’un échec de démarrage du processus se trouve également dans le Journal des événements de l’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-175">The cause of a process startup failure is also found in the Application Event Log.</span></span>

### <a name="50032-ancm-failed-to-load-dll"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-176">500.32 - Échec du chargement de la dll par ANCM</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-176">500.32 ANCM Failed to Load dll</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-177">Le processus de travail échoue.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-177">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-178">L’application ne démarre pas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-178">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-179">Le plus souvent, cette erreur provient du fait que l’application est publiée pour une architecture de processeur incompatible.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-179">The most common cause for this error is that the app is published for an incompatible processor architecture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-180">Si le processus de travail s’exécute en tant qu’application 32 bits et si l’application a été publiée pour cibler une architecture 64 bits, cette erreur se produit.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-180">If the worker process is running as a 32-bit app and the app was published to target 64-bit, this error occurs.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-181">Pour corriger cette erreur, vous avez le choix entre plusieurs possibilités :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-181">To fix this error, either:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-182">Republiez l’application pour la même architecture de processeur que celle du processus de travail.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-182">Republish the app for the same processor architecture as the worker process.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-183">Publiez l’application sous forme de [déploiement dépendant du framework](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-executables-fde).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-183">Publish the app as a [framework-dependent deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-executables-fde).</span></span>

### <a name="50033-ancm-request-handler-load-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-184">500.33 - Échec du chargement du gestionnaire de requêtes ANCM</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-184">500.33 ANCM Request Handler Load Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-185">Le processus de travail échoue.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-185">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-186">L’application ne démarre pas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-186">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-187">L’application n’a pas référencé le framework `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-187">The app didn't reference the `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App` framework.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-188">Seules les applications `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App` ciblant le cadre peuvent être hébergées par le [module de base ASP.NET](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-188">Only apps targeting the `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App` framework can be hosted by the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-189">Pour corriger cette erreur, vérifiez que l’application cible le framework `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-189">To fix this error, confirm that the app is targeting the `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App` framework.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-190">Examinez le fichier `.runtimeconfig.json` pour vérifier le framework ciblé par l’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-190">Check the `.runtimeconfig.json` to verify the framework targeted by the app.</span></span>

### <a name="50034-ancm-mixed-hosting-models-not-supported"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-191">500.34 - Modèles d’hébergement mixtes ANCM non pris en charge</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-191">500.34 ANCM Mixed Hosting Models Not Supported</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-192">Le processus de travail ne peut pas exécuter à la fois une application in-process et une application out-of-process dans le même processus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-192">The worker process can't run both an in-process app and an out-of-process app in the same process.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-193">Pour corriger cette erreur, exécutez les applications dans des pools d’applications IIS distincts.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-193">To fix this error, run apps in separate IIS application pools.</span></span>

### <a name="50035-ancm-multiple-in-process-applications-in-same-process"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-194">500.35 - Applications in-process multiples dans le même processus ANCM</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-194">500.35 ANCM Multiple In-Process Applications in same Process</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-195">Le processus de travail ne peut pas exécuter plusieurs applications en cours dans le même processus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-195">The worker process can't run multiple in-process apps in the same process.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-196">Pour corriger cette erreur, exécutez les applications dans des pools d’applications IIS distincts.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-196">To fix this error, run apps in separate IIS application pools.</span></span>

### <a name="50036-ancm-out-of-process-handler-load-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-197">500.36 - Échec de chargement du gestionnaire out-of-process ANCM</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-197">500.36 ANCM Out-Of-Process Handler Load Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-198">Le gestionnaire de requêtes out-of-process, *aspnetcorev2_outofprocess.dll*, ne se trouve pas aux côtés du fichier *aspnetcorev2.dll*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-198">The out-of-process request handler, *aspnetcorev2_outofprocess.dll*, isn't next to the *aspnetcorev2.dll* file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-199">Cela indique une installation corrompue du [module de base ASP.NET](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-199">This indicates a corrupted installation of the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-200">Pour corriger cette erreur, réparez l’installation du [bundle d’hébergement .NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#install-the-net-core-hosting-bundle) (pour IIS) ou Visual Studio (pour IIS Express).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-200">To fix this error, repair the installation of the [.NET Core Hosting Bundle](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#install-the-net-core-hosting-bundle) (for IIS) or Visual Studio (for IIS Express).</span></span>

### <a name="50037-ancm-failed-to-start-within-startup-time-limit"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-201">500.37 - Échec du démarrage d’ANCM dans le délai imparti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-201">500.37 ANCM Failed to Start Within Startup Time Limit</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-202">ANCM n’a pas pu démarrer dans le délai imparti spécifié.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-202">ANCM failed to start within the provied startup time limit.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-203">Par défaut, le délai d’expiration est de 120 secondes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-203">By default, the timeout is 120 seconds.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-204">Cette erreur peut se produire quand un grand nombre d’applications démarrent sur la même machine.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-204">This error can occur when starting a large number of apps on the same machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-205">Recherchez les pics d’utilisation du processeur/de la mémoire sur le serveur durant le démarrage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-205">Check for CPU/Memory usage spikes on the server during startup.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-206">Vous devrez peut-être décaler le processus de démarrage de plusieurs applications.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-206">You may need to stagger the startup process of multiple apps.</span></span>

### <a name="50038-ancm-application-dll-not-found"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-207">500.38 AnCM Application DLL Non trouvé</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-207">500.38 ANCM Application DLL Not Found</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-208">ANCM n’a pas réussi à localiser l’application DLL, qui devrait être à côté de l’exécutable.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-208">ANCM failed to locate the application DLL, which should be next to the executable.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-209">Cette erreur se produit lors de l’hébergement d’une application emballée comme un [fichier unique exécutable](/dotnet/core/whats-new/dotnet-core-3-0#single-file-executables) à l’aide du modèle d’hébergement en cours.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-209">This error occurs when hosting an app packaged as a [single-file executable](/dotnet/core/whats-new/dotnet-core-3-0#single-file-executables) using the in-process hosting model.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-210">Le modèle en cours exige que l’ANCM charge l’application .NET Core dans le processus IIS existant.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-210">The in-process model requires that the ANCM load the .NET Core app into the existing IIS process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-211">Ce scénario n’est pas pris en charge par le modèle de déploiement d’un seul fichier.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-211">This scenario isn't supported by the single-file deployment model.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-212">Utilisez **l’une** des approches suivantes dans le fichier de projet de l’application pour corriger cette erreur :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-212">Use **one** of the following approaches in the app's project file to fix this error:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-213">Désactiver la publication à un `PublishSingleFile` seul fichier en `false`fixant la propriété MSBuild à .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-213">Disable single-file publishing by setting the `PublishSingleFile` MSBuild property to `false`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-214">Passez au modèle d’hébergement hors-processus `AspNetCoreHostingModel` en définissant `OutOfProcess`la propriété MSBuild à .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-214">Switch to the out-of-process hosting model by setting the `AspNetCoreHostingModel` MSBuild property to `OutOfProcess`.</span></span>

### <a name="5025-process-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-215">Échec de processus 502.5</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-215">502.5 Process Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-216">Le processus de travail échoue.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-216">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-217">L’application ne démarre pas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-217">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-218">Le [module ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) tente, en vain, de démarrer le processus de travail.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-218">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) attempts to start the worker process but it fails to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-219">Vous pouvez généralement déterminer la cause d’un échec de démarrage du processus à partir des entrées du Journal des événements de l’application et du journal stdout du module ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-219">The cause of a process startup failure can usually be determined from entries in the Application Event Log and the ASP.NET Core Module stdout log.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-220">Une condition d’échec courante est une application mal configurée qui cible une version du framework partagé ASP.NET Core non présente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-220">A common failure condition is the app is misconfigured due to targeting a version of the ASP.NET Core shared framework that isn't present.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-221">Vérifiez les versions du framework partagé ASP.NET Core qui sont installées sur l’ordinateur cible.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-221">Check which versions of the ASP.NET Core shared framework are installed on the target machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-222">Le *framework partagé* est le jeu d’assemblys (fichiers *.dll*) qui sont installés sur l’ordinateur et référencés par un métapaquet comme `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-222">The *shared framework* is the set of assemblies (*.dll* files) that are installed on the machine and referenced by a metapackage such as `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-223">La référence de métapaquet peut spécifier une version minimale requise.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-223">The metapackage reference can specify a minimum required version.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-224">Pour plus d’informations, consultez [Le framework partagé](https://natemcmaster.com/blog/2018/08/29/netcore-primitives-2/).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-224">For more information, see [The shared framework](https://natemcmaster.com/blog/2018/08/29/netcore-primitives-2/).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-225">La page d’erreur d’un *échec de processus 502.5* est retournée quand une erreur de configuration d’hébergement ou d’application entraîne l’échec du processus de travail :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-225">The *502.5 Process Failure* error page is returned when a hosting or app misconfiguration causes the worker process to fail:</span></span>

### <a name="failed-to-start-application-errorcode-0x800700c1"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-226">Échec du démarrage de l’application (code d’erreur « 0x800700c1 »)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-226">Failed to start application (ErrorCode '0x800700c1')</span></span>

```
EventID: 1010
Source: IIS AspNetCore Module V2
Failed to start application '/LM/W3SVC/6/ROOT/', ErrorCode '0x800700c1'.
```

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-227">L’application n’a pas pu démarrer, car l’assembly de l’application (*.dll*) n’a pas pu être chargé.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-227">The app failed to start because the app's assembly (*.dll*) couldn't be loaded.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-228">Cette erreur se produit lorsqu’il existe une incompatibilité au niveau du nombre de bits entre l’application publiée et le processus w3wp/iisexpress.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-228">This error occurs when there's a bitness mismatch between the published app and the w3wp/iisexpress process.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-229">Vérifiez que le paramètre 32 bits du pool d’applications est correct :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-229">Confirm that the app pool's 32-bit setting is correct:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-230">Sélectionnez le pool d’applications parmi les **Pools d’applications** IIS Manager.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-230">Select the app pool in IIS Manager's **Application Pools**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-231">Sélectionnez **Paramètres avancés** sous **Modifier le pool d’applications** dans le volet **Actions**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-231">Select **Advanced Settings** under **Edit Application Pool** in the **Actions** panel.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-232">Définissez **Activer les applications 32 bits** :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-232">Set **Enable 32-Bit Applications**:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-233">Si vous déployez une application 32 bits (x86), définissez la valeur sur `True`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-233">If deploying a 32-bit (x86) app, set the value to `True`.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-234">Si vous déployez une application 64 bits (x64), définissez la valeur sur `False`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-234">If deploying a 64-bit (x64) app, set the value to `False`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-235">Confirmez qu’il n’y `<Platform>` a pas de conflit entre une propriété MSBuild dans le fichier du projet et la bitness publiée de l’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-235">Confirm that there isn't a conflict between a `<Platform>` MSBuild property in the project file and the published bitness of the app.</span></span>

### <a name="connection-reset"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-236">Réinitialisation de la connexion</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-236">Connection reset</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-237">Si une erreur se produit après l’envoi des en-têtes, il est trop tard pour que le serveur puisse envoyer une **erreur de serveur interne 500**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-237">If an error occurs after the headers are sent, it's too late for the server to send a **500 Internal Server Error** when an error occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-238">C’est souvent le cas quand une erreur se produit pendant la sérialisation des objets complexes d’une réponse.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-238">This often happens when an error occurs during the serialization of complex objects for a response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-239">Ce type d’erreur apparaît en tant qu’erreur de *réinitialisation de la connexion* sur le client.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-239">This type of error appears as a *connection reset* error on the client.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-240">La [journalisation des applications](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) peut aider à le résoudre.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-240">[Application logging](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) can help troubleshoot these types of errors.</span></span>

### <a name="default-startup-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-241">Limites de démarrage par défaut</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-241">Default startup limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-242">Le [module de base ASP.NET](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) est configuré avec une startup par *défautTimeLimit* de 120 secondes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-242">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) is configured with a default *startupTimeLimit* of 120 seconds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-243">Quand cette valeur par défaut est conservée, une application peut mettre jusqu’à deux minutes à démarrer avant que le module ne consigne un échec de processus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-243">When left at the default value, an app may take up to two minutes to start before the module logs a process failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-244">Pour plus d’informations sur la configuration du module, voir [Attributs de l’élément aspNetCore](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#attributes-of-the-aspnetcore-element).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-244">For information on configuring the module, see [Attributes of the aspNetCore element](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#attributes-of-the-aspnetcore-element).</span></span>

## <a name="troubleshoot-on-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-245">Dépannage sur Azure App Service</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-245">Troubleshoot on Azure App Service</span></span>

[!INCLUDE [Azure App Service Preview Notice](~/includes/azure-apps-preview-notice.md)]

### <a name="application-event-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-246">Journal d’événements d’application (Azure App Service)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-246">Application Event Log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-247">Pour accéder au Journal des événements de l’application, utilisez le panneau **Diagnostiquer et résoudre les problèmes** du Portail Azure :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-247">To access the Application Event Log, use the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade in the Azure portal:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-248">Dans le Portail Azure, ouvrez l’application dans **App Services**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-248">In the Azure portal, open the app in **App Services**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-249">Sélectionnez **Diagnostiquer et résoudre les problèmes**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-249">Select **Diagnose and solve problems**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-250">Sélectionnez le titre **Outils de diagnostic**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-250">Select the **Diagnostic Tools** heading.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-251">Sous **Outils de support**, sélectionnez le bouton **Événements d’application**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-251">Under **Support Tools**, select the **Application Events** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-252">Examinez la dernière erreur fournie par l’entrée *IIS AspNetCoreModule* ou *IIS AspNetCoreModule V2* dans la colonne **Source**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-252">Examine the latest error provided by the *IIS AspNetCoreModule* or *IIS AspNetCoreModule V2* entry in the **Source** column.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-253">En dehors de la solution consistant à utiliser le panneau **Diagnostiquer et résoudre les problèmes**, vous pouvez examiner directement le fichier Journal des événements de l’application avec [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki) :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-253">An alternative to using the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade is to examine the Application Event Log file directly using [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-254">Ouvrez les **Outils avancés** dans la zone **Outils de développement**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-254">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-255">Sélectionnez le bouton **Atteindre&rarr;**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-255">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-256">La console Kudu s’ouvre dans un nouvel onglet ou une nouvelle fenêtre du navigateur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-256">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-257">Dans la barre de navigation en haut de la page, ouvrez **Console de débogage** et sélectionnez **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-257">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-258">Ouvrez le fichier **LogFiles** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-258">Open the **LogFiles** folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-259">Sélectionnez l’icône en forme de crayon à côté du fichier *eventlog.xml*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-259">Select the pencil icon next to the *eventlog.xml* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-260">Examinez le journal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-260">Examine the log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-261">Allez en bas du journal pour voir les événements les plus récents.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-261">Scroll to the bottom of the log to see the most recent events.</span></span>

### <a name="run-the-app-in-the-kudu-console"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-262">Exécuter l’application dans la console Kudu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-262">Run the app in the Kudu console</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-263">De nombreuses erreurs de démarrage ne produisent pas d’informations utiles dans le Journal des événements de l’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-263">Many startup errors don't produce useful information in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-264">Vous pouvez exécuter l’application dans la console d’exécution à distance [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki) pour détecter l’erreur :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-264">You can run the app in the [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki) Remote Execution Console to discover the error:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-268">Dans la barre de navigation en haut de la page, ouvrez **Console de débogage** et sélectionnez **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-268">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>

#### <a name="test-a-32-bit-x86-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-269">Tester une application 32 bits (x86)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-269">Test a 32-bit (x86) app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-270">**Version actuelle**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-270">**Current release**</span></span>

1. `cd d:\home\site\wwwroot`
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-271">Exécutez l’application :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-271">Run the app:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-272">Si l’application est un [déploiement dépendant du framework](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd) :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-272">If the app is a [framework-dependent deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span></span>

     ```dotnetcli
     dotnet .\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll
     ```

   * <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-273">Si l’application est un [déploiement autonome](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd) :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-273">If the app is a [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span></span>

     ```console
     {ASSEMBLY NAME}.exe
     ```

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-274">La sortie de console de l’application, affichant toutes les erreurs éventuelles, est transmise à la console Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-274">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-275">**Déploiement dépendant du framework sur une préversion**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-275">**Framework-dependent deployment running on a preview release**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-276">*Installation de l’extension de site du runtime ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x86) requise.*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-276">*Requires installing the ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x86) Runtime site extension.*</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-277">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x32` (`{X.Y}` est la version du runtime).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-277">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x32` (`{X.Y}` is the runtime version)</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-278">Exécutez l'application : `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-278">Run the app: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-279">La sortie de console de l’application, affichant toutes les erreurs éventuelles, est transmise à la console Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-279">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-stdout-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-292">ASP.NET Core Module stdout log (Azure App Service)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-292">ASP.NET Core Module stdout log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-293">Le journal stdout du module ASP.NET Core enregistre souvent des messages d’erreur utiles et absents du Journal des événements de l’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-293">The ASP.NET Core Module stdout log often records useful error messages not found in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-294">Pour activer et afficher les journaux stdout :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-294">To enable and view stdout logs:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-295">Accédez au panneau **Diagnostiquer et résoudre les problèmes** du Portail Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-295">Navigate to the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade in the Azure portal.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-296">Sous **SÉLECTIONNER UNE CATÉGORIE DE PROBLÈME**, sélectionnez le bouton **Application web en panne**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-296">Under **SELECT PROBLEM CATEGORY**, select the **Web App Down** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-297">Sous **Solutions suggérées** > **Activer la redirection de journaux stdout**, sélectionnez le bouton **Ouvrir la console Kudu pour modifier web.config**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-297">Under **Suggested Solutions** > **Enable Stdout Log Redirection**, select the button to **Open Kudu Console to edit Web.Config**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-298">Dans la **Console de diagnostic** Kudu, ouvrez les dossiers sur le chemin d’accès **site** > **wwwroot**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-298">In the Kudu **Diagnostic Console**, open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-299">Faites défiler la page jusqu’à révéler le fichier *web.config* en bas de la liste.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-299">Scroll down to reveal the *web.config* file at the bottom of the list.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-300">Cliquez sur l’icône en forme de crayon à côté du fichier *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-300">Click the pencil icon next to the *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-301">Définissez **stdoutLogEnabled** sur `true` et remplacez le chemin **stdoutLogFile** par : `\\?\%home%\LogFiles\stdout`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-301">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `true` and change the **stdoutLogFile** path to: `\\?\%home%\LogFiles\stdout`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-302">Sélectionnez **Enregistrer** pour enregistrer le fichier *web.config* mis à jour.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-302">Select **Save** to save the updated *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-303">Adressez une requête à l’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-303">Make a request to the app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-304">Revenez au Portail Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-304">Return to the Azure portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-305">Sélectionnez le panneau **Outils avancés** dans la zone **OUTILS DE DÉVELOPPEMENT**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-305">Select the **Advanced Tools** blade in the **DEVELOPMENT TOOLS** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-306">Sélectionnez le bouton **Atteindre&rarr;**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-306">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-307">La console Kudu s’ouvre dans un nouvel onglet ou une nouvelle fenêtre du navigateur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-307">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-308">Dans la barre de navigation en haut de la page, ouvrez **Console de débogage** et sélectionnez **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-308">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-309">Sélectionnez le dossier **LogFiles**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-309">Select the **LogFiles** folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-310">Inspectez la colonne **Modifié** et sélectionnez l’icône en forme de crayon pour modifier le journal stdout avec la date de dernière modification.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-310">Inspect the **Modified** column and select the pencil icon to edit the stdout log with the latest modification date.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-311">Lorsque le fichier journal s’ouvre, l’erreur s’affiche.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-311">When the log file opens, the error is displayed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-312">Désactivez la journalisation stdout, une fois les problèmes résolus :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-312">Disable stdout logging when troubleshooting is complete:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-313">Dans la **Console de diagnostic** Kudu, revenez au chemin d’accès **site** > **wwwroot** pour faire apparaître le fichier *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-313">In the Kudu **Diagnostic Console**, return to the path **site** > **wwwroot** to reveal the *web.config* file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-314">Ouvrez à nouveau le fichier **web.config** en sélectionnant l’icône en forme de crayon.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-314">Open the **web.config** file again by selecting the pencil icon.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-315">Définissez **stdoutLogEnabled** sur `false`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-315">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `false`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-316">Sélectionnez **Enregistrer** pour enregistrer le fichier.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-316">Select **Save** to save the file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-317">Pour plus d’informations, consultez <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-317">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-318">Si vous ne désactivez pas le journal stdout, l’application ou le serveur risque d’échouer.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-318">Failure to disable the stdout log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-319">Il n’existe aucune limite quant à la taille du fichier journal ou au nombre de fichiers journaux créés.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-319">There's no limit on log file size or the number of log files created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-320">N’utilisez la journalisation stdout que pour résoudre les problèmes de démarrage de l’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-320">Only use stdout logging to troubleshoot app startup problems.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-321">Pour la journalisation générale dans une application ASP.NET Core après le démarrage, utilisez une bibliothèque de journalisation qui limite la taille du fichier journal et applique une rotation aux journaux.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-321">For general logging in an ASP.NET Core app after startup, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-322">Pour plus d’informations, consultez [Fournisseurs de journalisation tiers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-322">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-debug-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-323">ASP.NET Journal de débbu de module de base (Azure App Service)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-323">ASP.NET Core Module debug log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-324">Le journal de débogage du module ASP.NET Core fournit une journalisation supplémentaire, plus approfondie, à partir du module ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-324">The ASP.NET Core Module debug log provides additional, deeper logging from the ASP.NET Core Module.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-325">Pour activer et afficher les journaux stdout :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-325">To enable and view stdout logs:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-326">Pour activer le journal de diagnostic amélioré, effectuez l’une des opérations suivantes :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-326">To enable the enhanced diagnostic log, perform either of the following:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-327">Suivez les instructions indiquées dans [Journaux de diagnostic améliorés](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs) afin de configurer l’application pour une journalisation des diagnostics améliorée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-327">Follow the instructions in [Enhanced diagnostic logs](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs) to configure the app for an enhanced diagnostic logging.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-328">Redéployez l’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-328">Redeploy the app.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-329">Ajoutez le `<handlerSettings>` présenté dans [Journaux de diagnostic améliorés](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs) au fichier *web.config* de l’application en production à l’aide de la console Kudu :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-329">Add the `<handlerSettings>` shown in [Enhanced diagnostic logs](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs) to the live app's *web.config* file using the Kudu console:</span></span>
     1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-330">Ouvrez les **Outils avancés** dans la zone **Outils de développement**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-330">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-331">Sélectionnez le bouton **Atteindre&rarr;**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-331">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-332">La console Kudu s’ouvre dans un nouvel onglet ou une nouvelle fenêtre du navigateur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-332">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
     1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-333">Dans la barre de navigation en haut de la page, ouvrez **Console de débogage** et sélectionnez **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-333">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>
     1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-334">Ouvrez les dossiers sur le **site** > **wwwroot**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-334">Open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-335">Modifiez le fichier *web.config* en sélectionnant le bouton représentant un crayon.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-335">Edit the *web.config* file by selecting the pencil button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-336">Ajoutez la section `<handlerSettings>` comme indiqué dans [Journaux de diagnostic améliorés](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-336">Add the `<handlerSettings>` section as shown in [Enhanced diagnostic logs](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-337">Sélectionnez le bouton **Enregistrer**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-337">Select the **Save** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-338">Ouvrez les **Outils avancés** dans la zone **Outils de développement**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-338">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-339">Sélectionnez le bouton **Atteindre&rarr;**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-339">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-340">La console Kudu s’ouvre dans un nouvel onglet ou une nouvelle fenêtre du navigateur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-340">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-341">Dans la barre de navigation en haut de la page, ouvrez **Console de débogage** et sélectionnez **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-341">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-342">Ouvrez les dossiers sur le **site** > **wwwroot**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-342">Open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-343">Si vous n’avez pas indiqué de chemin pour le fichier *aspnetcore-debug.log*, le fichier apparaît dans la liste.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-343">If you didn't supply a path for the *aspnetcore-debug.log* file, the file appears in the list.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-344">Si vous avez indiqué un chemin, accédez à l’emplacement du fichier journal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-344">If you supplied a path, navigate to the location of the log file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-345">Ouvrez le fichier journal à l’aide du bouton représentant un crayon à côté du nom de fichier.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-345">Open the log file with the pencil button next to the file name.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-346">Désactivez la journalisation du débogage, une fois la résolution des problèmes effectuée :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-346">Disable debug logging when troubleshooting is complete:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-347">Pour désactiver la journalisation de débogage améliorée, effectuez l’une des opérations suivantes :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-347">To disable the enhanced debug log, perform either of the following:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-348">Supprimez `<handlerSettings>` du fichier *web.config* localement, puis redéployez l’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-348">Remove the `<handlerSettings>` from the *web.config* file locally and redeploy the app.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-349">Utilisez la console Kudu pour modifier le fichier *web.config* et supprimer la section `<handlerSettings>`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-349">Use the Kudu console to edit the *web.config* file and remove the `<handlerSettings>` section.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-350">Enregistrez le fichier .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-350">Save the file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-351">Pour plus d’informations, consultez <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-351">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs>.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-352">Si le journal de débogage n’est pas désactivé, cela peut entraîner une défaillance de l’application ou du serveur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-352">Failure to disable the debug log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-353">Il n’existe aucune limite à la taille du fichier journal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-353">There's no limit on log file size.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-354">Utilisez uniquement la journalisation de débogage pour résoudre les problèmes de démarrage d’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-354">Only use debug logging to troubleshoot app startup problems.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-355">Pour la journalisation générale dans une application ASP.NET Core après le démarrage, utilisez une bibliothèque de journalisation qui limite la taille du fichier journal et applique une rotation aux journaux.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-355">For general logging in an ASP.NET Core app after startup, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-356">Pour plus d’informations, consultez [Fournisseurs de journalisation tiers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-356">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

### <a name="slow-or-hanging-app-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-357">Application lente ou suspendue (Azure App Service)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-357">Slow or hanging app (Azure App Service)</span></span>
