## <a name="app-startup-errors"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-526">Erreurs de démarrage des applications</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-526">App startup errors</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-527">Dans Visual Studio, un projet ASP.NET Core est par défaut hébergé sur [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview) pendant une opération de débogage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-527">In Visual Studio, an ASP.NET Core project defaults to [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview) hosting during debugging.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-528">Un *502.5 - Échec du processus* ou un *500.30 - Échec de démarrage* qui se produit lors de débogage localement peut être diagnostiqué en utilisant les conseils dans ce sujet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-528">A *502.5 - Process Failure* or a *500.30 - Start Failure* that occurs when debugging locally can be diagnosed using the advice in this topic.</span></span>

### <a name="40314-forbidden"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-529">403.14 Interdit</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-529">403.14 Forbidden</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-530">L’application ne démarre pas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-530">The app fails to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-531">L’erreur suivante est enregistrée :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-531">The following error is logged:</span></span>

```
The Web server is configured to not list the contents of this directory.
```

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-532">L’erreur est généralement causée par un déploiement interrompu sur le système d’hébergement, qui comprend l’un des scénarios suivants:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-532">The error is usually caused by a broken deployment on the hosting system, which includes any of the following scenarios:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-533">L’application est déployée dans le mauvais dossier sur le système d’hébergement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-533">The app is deployed to the wrong folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-534">Le processus de déploiement n’a pas permis de transférer tous les fichiers et dossiers de l’application dans le dossier de déploiement du système d’hébergement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-534">The deployment process failed to move all of the app's files and folders to the deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-535">Le fichier *web.config* est absent du déploiement, ou le contenu du fichier *web.config* sont malformés.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-535">The *web.config* file is missing from the deployment, or the *web.config* file contents are malformed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-536">Procédez comme suit :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-536">Perform the following steps:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-537">Supprimer tous les fichiers et dossiers du dossier de déploiement sur le système d’hébergement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-537">Delete all of the files and folders from the deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-538">Redéployez le contenu du dossier de *publication* de l’application sur le système d’hébergement en utilisant votre méthode normale de déploiement, comme Visual Studio, PowerShell ou déploiement manuel :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-538">Redeploy the contents of the app's *publish* folder to the hosting system using your normal method of deployment, such as Visual Studio, PowerShell, or manual deployment:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-539">Confirmez que le fichier *web.config* est présent dans le déploiement et que son contenu est correct.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-539">Confirm that the *web.config* file is present in the deployment and that its contents are correct.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-540">Lors de l’hébergement sur Azure App Service, confirmez que l’application est déployée dans le `D:\home\site\wwwroot` dossier.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-540">When hosting on Azure App Service, confirm that the app is deployed to the `D:\home\site\wwwroot` folder.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-541">Lorsque l’application est hébergée par l’IIS, confirmez que l’application est déployée sur le **chemin physique** de l’IIS indiqué dans **les paramètres**de base de **l’IIS Manager**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-541">When the app is hosted by IIS, confirm that the app is deployed to the IIS **Physical path** shown in **IIS Manager**'s **Basic Settings**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-542">Confirmez que tous les fichiers et dossiers de l’application sont déployés en comparant le déploiement sur le système d’hébergement au contenu du dossier de *publication* du projet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-542">Confirm that all of the app's files and folders are deployed by comparing the deployment on the hosting system to the contents of the project's *publish* folder.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-543">Pour plus d’informations sur la mise en page <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>d’une application ASP.NET Core publiée, voir .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-543">For more information on the layout of a published ASP.NET Core app, see <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-544">Pour plus d’informations sur le <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#configuration-with-webconfig>fichier *web.config,* voir .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-544">For more information on the *web.config* file, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#configuration-with-webconfig>.</span></span>

### <a name="500-internal-server-error"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-545">500 Erreur interne du serveur</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-545">500 Internal Server Error</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-546">L’application démarre, mais une erreur empêche le serveur de répondre à la requête.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-546">The app starts, but an error prevents the server from fulfilling the request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-547">Cette erreur se produit dans le code de l’application pendant le démarrage ou durant la création d’une réponse.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-547">This error occurs within the app's code during startup or while creating a response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-548">La réponse peut être dépourvue de contenu ou apparaître sous la forme d’une *erreur de serveur interne 500* dans le navigateur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-548">The response may contain no content, or the response may appear as a *500 Internal Server Error* in the browser.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-549">Le Journal des événements de l’application indique généralement qu’elle a démarré normalement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-549">The Application Event Log usually states that the app started normally.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-550">Du point de vue du serveur, c’est exact.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-550">From the server's perspective, that's correct.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-551">L’application a démarré, mais elle ne peut pas générer de réponse valide.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-551">The app did start, but it can't generate a valid response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-552">Exécutez l’application depuis une invite de commandes sur le serveur ou activez le journal stdout du module ASP.NET Core pour résoudre le problème.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-552">Run the app at a command prompt on the server or enable the ASP.NET Core Module stdout log to troubleshoot the problem.</span></span>

### <a name="5000-in-process-handler-load-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-553">500.0 - Échec de chargement du gestionnaire in-process</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-553">500.0 In-Process Handler Load Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-554">Le processus de travail échoue.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-554">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-555">L’application ne démarre pas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-555">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-556">Le [module de base ASP.NET](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) ne parvient pas à trouver le CLR de base .NET et à trouver le gestionnaire de demande en cours (*aspnetcorev2_inprocess.dll*).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-556">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) fails to find the .NET Core CLR and find the in-process request handler (*aspnetcorev2_inprocess.dll*).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-557">Vérifiez les éléments suivants :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-557">Check that:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-558">l’application cible le package NuGet [Microsoft.AspNetCore.Server.IIS](https://www.nuget.org/packages/Microsoft.AspNetCore.Server.IIS) ou le [métapaquet Microsoft.AspNetCore.App](xref:fundamentals/metapackage-app) ;</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-558">The app targets either the [Microsoft.AspNetCore.Server.IIS](https://www.nuget.org/packages/Microsoft.AspNetCore.Server.IIS) NuGet package or the [Microsoft.AspNetCore.App metapackage](xref:fundamentals/metapackage-app).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-559">la version du framework partagé ASP.NET Core que l’application cible est installée sur l’ordinateur cible.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-559">The version of the ASP.NET Core shared framework that the app targets is installed on the target machine.</span></span>

### <a name="5000-out-of-process-handler-load-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-560">500.0 - Échec de chargement du gestionnaire out-of-process</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-560">500.0 Out-Of-Process Handler Load Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-561">Le processus de travail échoue.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-561">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-562">L’application ne démarre pas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-562">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-563">Le [ASP.NET module de base](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) ne parvient pas à trouver le gestionnaire de demande d’hébergement hors-processus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-563">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) fails to find the out-of-process hosting request handler.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-564">Vérifiez que le fichier *aspnetcorev2_outofprocess.dll* est présent dans un sous-dossier en regard de *aspnetcorev2.dll*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-564">Make sure the *aspnetcorev2_outofprocess.dll* is present in a subfolder next to *aspnetcorev2.dll*.</span></span>

### <a name="5025-process-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-565">Échec de processus 502.5</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-565">502.5 Process Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-566">Le processus de travail échoue.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-566">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-567">L’application ne démarre pas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-567">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-568">Le [module ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) tente, en vain, de démarrer le processus de travail.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-568">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) attempts to start the worker process but it fails to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-569">Vous pouvez généralement déterminer la cause d’un échec de démarrage du processus à partir des entrées du Journal des événements de l’application et du journal stdout du module ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-569">The cause of a process startup failure can usually be determined from entries in the Application Event Log and the ASP.NET Core Module stdout log.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-570">Une condition d’échec courante est une application mal configurée qui cible une version du framework partagé ASP.NET Core non présente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-570">A common failure condition is the app is misconfigured due to targeting a version of the ASP.NET Core shared framework that isn't present.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-571">Vérifiez les versions du framework partagé ASP.NET Core qui sont installées sur l’ordinateur cible.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-571">Check which versions of the ASP.NET Core shared framework are installed on the target machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-572">Le *framework partagé* est le jeu d’assemblys (fichiers *.dll*) qui sont installés sur l’ordinateur et référencés par un métapaquet comme `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-572">The *shared framework* is the set of assemblies (*.dll* files) that are installed on the machine and referenced by a metapackage such as `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-573">La référence de métapaquet peut spécifier une version minimale requise.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-573">The metapackage reference can specify a minimum required version.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-574">Pour plus d’informations, consultez [Le framework partagé](https://natemcmaster.com/blog/2018/08/29/netcore-primitives-2/).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-574">For more information, see [The shared framework](https://natemcmaster.com/blog/2018/08/29/netcore-primitives-2/).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-575">La page d’erreur d’un *échec de processus 502.5* est retournée quand une erreur de configuration d’hébergement ou d’application entraîne l’échec du processus de travail :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-575">The *502.5 Process Failure* error page is returned when a hosting or app misconfiguration causes the worker process to fail:</span></span>

### <a name="failed-to-start-application-errorcode-0x800700c1"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-576">Échec du démarrage de l’application (code d’erreur « 0x800700c1 »)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-576">Failed to start application (ErrorCode '0x800700c1')</span></span>

```
EventID: 1010
Source: IIS AspNetCore Module V2
Failed to start application '/LM/W3SVC/6/ROOT/', ErrorCode '0x800700c1'.
```

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-577">L’application n’a pas pu démarrer, car l’assembly de l’application (*.dll*) n’a pas pu être chargé.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-577">The app failed to start because the app's assembly (*.dll*) couldn't be loaded.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-578">Cette erreur se produit lorsqu’il existe une incompatibilité au niveau du nombre de bits entre l’application publiée et le processus w3wp/iisexpress.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-578">This error occurs when there's a bitness mismatch between the published app and the w3wp/iisexpress process.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-579">Vérifiez que le paramètre 32 bits du pool d’applications est correct :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-579">Confirm that the app pool's 32-bit setting is correct:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-580">Sélectionnez le pool d’applications parmi les **Pools d’applications** IIS Manager.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-580">Select the app pool in IIS Manager's **Application Pools**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-581">Sélectionnez **Paramètres avancés** sous **Modifier le pool d’applications** dans le volet **Actions**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-581">Select **Advanced Settings** under **Edit Application Pool** in the **Actions** panel.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-582">Définissez **Activer les applications 32 bits** :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-582">Set **Enable 32-Bit Applications**:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-583">Si vous déployez une application 32 bits (x86), définissez la valeur sur `True`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-583">If deploying a 32-bit (x86) app, set the value to `True`.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-584">Si vous déployez une application 64 bits (x64), définissez la valeur sur `False`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-584">If deploying a 64-bit (x64) app, set the value to `False`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-585">Confirmez qu’il n’y `<Platform>` a pas de conflit entre une propriété MSBuild dans le fichier du projet et la bitness publiée de l’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-585">Confirm that there isn't a conflict between a `<Platform>` MSBuild property in the project file and the published bitness of the app.</span></span>

### <a name="connection-reset"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-586">Réinitialisation de la connexion</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-586">Connection reset</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-587">Si une erreur se produit après l’envoi des en-têtes, il est trop tard pour que le serveur puisse envoyer une **erreur de serveur interne 500**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-587">If an error occurs after the headers are sent, it's too late for the server to send a **500 Internal Server Error** when an error occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-588">C’est souvent le cas quand une erreur se produit pendant la sérialisation des objets complexes d’une réponse.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-588">This often happens when an error occurs during the serialization of complex objects for a response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-589">Ce type d’erreur apparaît en tant qu’erreur de *réinitialisation de la connexion* sur le client.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-589">This type of error appears as a *connection reset* error on the client.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-590">La [journalisation des applications](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) peut aider à le résoudre.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-590">[Application logging](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) can help troubleshoot these types of errors.</span></span>

### <a name="default-startup-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-591">Limites de démarrage par défaut</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-591">Default startup limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-592">Le [module de base ASP.NET](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) est configuré avec une startup par *défautTimeLimit* de 120 secondes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-592">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) is configured with a default *startupTimeLimit* of 120 seconds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-593">Quand cette valeur par défaut est conservée, une application peut mettre jusqu’à deux minutes à démarrer avant que le module ne consigne un échec de processus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-593">When left at the default value, an app may take up to two minutes to start before the module logs a process failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-594">Pour plus d’informations sur la configuration du module, voir [Attributs de l’élément aspNetCore](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#attributes-of-the-aspnetcore-element).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-594">For information on configuring the module, see [Attributes of the aspNetCore element](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#attributes-of-the-aspnetcore-element).</span></span>

## <a name="troubleshoot-on-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-595">Dépannage sur Azure App Service</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-595">Troubleshoot on Azure App Service</span></span>

[!INCLUDE [Azure App Service Preview Notice](~/includes/azure-apps-preview-notice.md)]

### <a name="application-event-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-596">Journal d’événements d’application (Azure App Service)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-596">Application Event Log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-597">Pour accéder au Journal des événements de l’application, utilisez le panneau **Diagnostiquer et résoudre les problèmes** du Portail Azure :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-597">To access the Application Event Log, use the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade in the Azure portal:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-598">Dans le Portail Azure, ouvrez l’application dans **App Services**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-598">In the Azure portal, open the app in **App Services**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-599">Sélectionnez **Diagnostiquer et résoudre les problèmes**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-599">Select **Diagnose and solve problems**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-600">Sélectionnez le titre **Outils de diagnostic**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-600">Select the **Diagnostic Tools** heading.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-601">Sous **Outils de support**, sélectionnez le bouton **Événements d’application**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-601">Under **Support Tools**, select the **Application Events** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-602">Examinez la dernière erreur fournie par l’entrée *IIS AspNetCoreModule* ou *IIS AspNetCoreModule V2* dans la colonne **Source**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-602">Examine the latest error provided by the *IIS AspNetCoreModule* or *IIS AspNetCoreModule V2* entry in the **Source** column.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-603">En dehors de la solution consistant à utiliser le panneau **Diagnostiquer et résoudre les problèmes**, vous pouvez examiner directement le fichier Journal des événements de l’application avec [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki) :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-603">An alternative to using the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade is to examine the Application Event Log file directly using [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-604">Ouvrez les **Outils avancés** dans la zone **Outils de développement**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-604">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-605">Sélectionnez le bouton **Atteindre&rarr;**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-605">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-606">La console Kudu s’ouvre dans un nouvel onglet ou une nouvelle fenêtre du navigateur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-606">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-607">Dans la barre de navigation en haut de la page, ouvrez **Console de débogage** et sélectionnez **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-607">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-608">Ouvrez le fichier **LogFiles** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-608">Open the **LogFiles** folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-609">Sélectionnez l’icône en forme de crayon à côté du fichier *eventlog.xml*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-609">Select the pencil icon next to the *eventlog.xml* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-610">Examinez le journal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-610">Examine the log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-611">Allez en bas du journal pour voir les événements les plus récents.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-611">Scroll to the bottom of the log to see the most recent events.</span></span>

### <a name="run-the-app-in-the-kudu-console"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-612">Exécuter l’application dans la console Kudu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-612">Run the app in the Kudu console</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-613">De nombreuses erreurs de démarrage ne produisent pas d’informations utiles dans le Journal des événements de l’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-613">Many startup errors don't produce useful information in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-614">Vous pouvez exécuter l’application dans la console d’exécution à distance [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki) pour détecter l’erreur :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-614">You can run the app in the [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki) Remote Execution Console to discover the error:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-615">Ouvrez les **Outils avancés** dans la zone **Outils de développement**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-615">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-616">Sélectionnez le bouton **Atteindre&rarr;**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-616">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-617">La console Kudu s’ouvre dans un nouvel onglet ou une nouvelle fenêtre du navigateur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-617">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-618">Dans la barre de navigation en haut de la page, ouvrez **Console de débogage** et sélectionnez **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-618">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>

#### <a name="test-a-32-bit-x86-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-619">Tester une application 32 bits (x86)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-619">Test a 32-bit (x86) app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-620">**Version actuelle**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-620">**Current release**</span></span>

1. `cd d:\home\site\wwwroot`
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-621">Exécutez l’application :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-621">Run the app:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-622">Si l’application est un [déploiement dépendant du framework](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd) :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-622">If the app is a [framework-dependent deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span></span>

     ```dotnetcli
     dotnet .\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll
     ```

   * <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-623">Si l’application est un [déploiement autonome](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd) :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-623">If the app is a [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span></span>

     ```console
     {ASSEMBLY NAME}.exe
     ```

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-624">La sortie de console de l’application, affichant toutes les erreurs éventuelles, est transmise à la console Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-624">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-625">**Déploiement dépendant du framework sur une préversion**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-625">**Framework-dependent deployment running on a preview release**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-626">*Installation de l’extension de site du runtime ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x86) requise.*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-626">*Requires installing the ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x86) Runtime site extension.*</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-627">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x32` (`{X.Y}` est la version du runtime).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-627">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x32` (`{X.Y}` is the runtime version)</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-628">Exécutez l'application : `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-628">Run the app: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-629">La sortie de console de l’application, affichant toutes les erreurs éventuelles, est transmise à la console Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-629">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

#### <a name="test-a-64-bit-x64-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-630">Tester une application 64 bits (x64)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-630">Test a 64-bit (x64) app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-631">**Version actuelle**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-631">**Current release**</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-632">Si l’application est un [déploiement dépendant du framework](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd) 64 bits (x64) :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-632">If the app is a 64-bit (x64) [framework-dependent deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span></span>
  1. `cd D:\Program Files\dotnet`
  1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-633">Exécutez l'application : `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-633">Run the app: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-634">Si l’application est un [déploiement autonome](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd) :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-634">If the app is a [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span></span>
  1. `cd D:\home\site\wwwroot`
  1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-635">Exécutez l'application : `{ASSEMBLY NAME}.exe`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-635">Run the app: `{ASSEMBLY NAME}.exe`</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-636">La sortie de console de l’application, affichant toutes les erreurs éventuelles, est transmise à la console Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-636">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-637">**Déploiement dépendant du framework sur une préversion**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-637">**Framework-dependent deployment running on a preview release**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-638">*Installation de l’extension de site du runtime ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x64) requise.*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-638">*Requires installing the ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x64) Runtime site extension.*</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-639">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x64` (`{X.Y}` est la version du runtime).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-639">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x64` (`{X.Y}` is the runtime version)</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-640">Exécutez l'application : `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-640">Run the app: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-641">La sortie de console de l’application, affichant toutes les erreurs éventuelles, est transmise à la console Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-641">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-stdout-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-642">ASP.NET Core Module stdout log (Azure App Service)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-642">ASP.NET Core Module stdout log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-643">Le journal stdout du module ASP.NET Core enregistre souvent des messages d’erreur utiles et absents du Journal des événements de l’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-643">The ASP.NET Core Module stdout log often records useful error messages not found in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-644">Pour activer et afficher les journaux stdout :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-644">To enable and view stdout logs:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-645">Accédez au panneau **Diagnostiquer et résoudre les problèmes** du Portail Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-645">Navigate to the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade in the Azure portal.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-646">Sous **SÉLECTIONNER UNE CATÉGORIE DE PROBLÈME**, sélectionnez le bouton **Application web en panne**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-646">Under **SELECT PROBLEM CATEGORY**, select the **Web App Down** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-647">Sous **Solutions suggérées** > **Activer la redirection de journaux stdout**, sélectionnez le bouton **Ouvrir la console Kudu pour modifier web.config**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-647">Under **Suggested Solutions** > **Enable Stdout Log Redirection**, select the button to **Open Kudu Console to edit Web.Config**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-648">Dans la **Console de diagnostic** Kudu, ouvrez les dossiers sur le chemin d’accès **site** > **wwwroot**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-648">In the Kudu **Diagnostic Console**, open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-649">Faites défiler la page jusqu’à révéler le fichier *web.config* en bas de la liste.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-649">Scroll down to reveal the *web.config* file at the bottom of the list.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-650">Cliquez sur l’icône en forme de crayon à côté du fichier *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-650">Click the pencil icon next to the *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-651">Définissez **stdoutLogEnabled** sur `true` et remplacez le chemin **stdoutLogFile** par : `\\?\%home%\LogFiles\stdout`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-651">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `true` and change the **stdoutLogFile** path to: `\\?\%home%\LogFiles\stdout`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-652">Sélectionnez **Enregistrer** pour enregistrer le fichier *web.config* mis à jour.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-652">Select **Save** to save the updated *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-653">Adressez une requête à l’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-653">Make a request to the app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-654">Revenez au Portail Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-654">Return to the Azure portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-655">Sélectionnez le panneau **Outils avancés** dans la zone **OUTILS DE DÉVELOPPEMENT**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-655">Select the **Advanced Tools** blade in the **DEVELOPMENT TOOLS** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-656">Sélectionnez le bouton **Atteindre&rarr;**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-656">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-657">La console Kudu s’ouvre dans un nouvel onglet ou une nouvelle fenêtre du navigateur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-657">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-658">Dans la barre de navigation en haut de la page, ouvrez **Console de débogage** et sélectionnez **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-658">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-659">Sélectionnez le dossier **LogFiles**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-659">Select the **LogFiles** folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-660">Inspectez la colonne **Modifié** et sélectionnez l’icône en forme de crayon pour modifier le journal stdout avec la date de dernière modification.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-660">Inspect the **Modified** column and select the pencil icon to edit the stdout log with the latest modification date.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-661">Lorsque le fichier journal s’ouvre, l’erreur s’affiche.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-661">When the log file opens, the error is displayed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-662">Désactivez la journalisation stdout, une fois les problèmes résolus :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-662">Disable stdout logging when troubleshooting is complete:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-663">Dans la **Console de diagnostic** Kudu, revenez au chemin d’accès **site** > **wwwroot** pour faire apparaître le fichier *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-663">In the Kudu **Diagnostic Console**, return to the path **site** > **wwwroot** to reveal the *web.config* file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-664">Ouvrez à nouveau le fichier **web.config** en sélectionnant l’icône en forme de crayon.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-664">Open the **web.config** file again by selecting the pencil icon.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-665">Définissez **stdoutLogEnabled** sur `false`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-665">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `false`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-666">Sélectionnez **Enregistrer** pour enregistrer le fichier.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-666">Select **Save** to save the file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-667">Pour plus d’informations, consultez <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-667">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-668">Si vous ne désactivez pas le journal stdout, l’application ou le serveur risque d’échouer.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-668">Failure to disable the stdout log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-669">Il n’existe aucune limite quant à la taille du fichier journal ou au nombre de fichiers journaux créés.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-669">There's no limit on log file size or the number of log files created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-670">N’utilisez la journalisation stdout que pour résoudre les problèmes de démarrage de l’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-670">Only use stdout logging to troubleshoot app startup problems.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-671">Pour la journalisation générale dans une application ASP.NET Core après le démarrage, utilisez une bibliothèque de journalisation qui limite la taille du fichier journal et applique une rotation aux journaux.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-671">For general logging in an ASP.NET Core app after startup, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-672">Pour plus d’informations, consultez [Fournisseurs de journalisation tiers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-672">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-debug-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-673">ASP.NET Journal de débbu de module de base (Azure App Service)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-673">ASP.NET Core Module debug log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-674">Le journal de débogage du module ASP.NET Core fournit une journalisation supplémentaire, plus approfondie, à partir du module ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-674">The ASP.NET Core Module debug log provides additional, deeper logging from the ASP.NET Core Module.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-675">Pour activer et afficher les journaux stdout :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-675">To enable and view stdout logs:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-676">Pour activer le journal de diagnostic amélioré, effectuez l’une des opérations suivantes :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-676">To enable the enhanced diagnostic log, perform either of the following:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-677">Suivez les instructions indiquées dans [Journaux de diagnostic améliorés](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs) afin de configurer l’application pour une journalisation des diagnostics améliorée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-677">Follow the instructions in [Enhanced diagnostic logs](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs) to configure the app for an enhanced diagnostic logging.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-678">Redéployez l’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-678">Redeploy the app.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-679">Ajoutez le `<handlerSettings>` présenté dans [Journaux de diagnostic améliorés](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs) au fichier *web.config* de l’application en production à l’aide de la console Kudu :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-679">Add the `<handlerSettings>` shown in [Enhanced diagnostic logs](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs) to the live app's *web.config* file using the Kudu console:</span></span>
     1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-680">Ouvrez les **Outils avancés** dans la zone **Outils de développement**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-680">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-681">Sélectionnez le bouton **Atteindre&rarr;**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-681">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-682">La console Kudu s’ouvre dans un nouvel onglet ou une nouvelle fenêtre du navigateur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-682">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>

     1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-684">Ouvrez les dossiers sur le **site** > **wwwroot**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-684">Open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-685">Modifiez le fichier *web.config* en sélectionnant le bouton représentant un crayon.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-685">Edit the *web.config* file by selecting the pencil button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-686">Ajoutez la section `<handlerSettings>` comme indiqué dans [Journaux de diagnostic améliorés](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-686">Add the `<handlerSettings>` section as shown in [Enhanced diagnostic logs](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-687">Sélectionnez le bouton **Enregistrer**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-687">Select the **Save** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-688">Ouvrez les **Outils avancés** dans la zone **Outils de développement**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-688">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-689">Sélectionnez le bouton **Atteindre&rarr;**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-689">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-690">La console Kudu s’ouvre dans un nouvel onglet ou une nouvelle fenêtre du navigateur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-690">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-691">Dans la barre de navigation en haut de la page, ouvrez **Console de débogage** et sélectionnez **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-691">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-692">Ouvrez les dossiers sur le **site** > **wwwroot**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-692">Open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-693">Si vous n’avez pas indiqué de chemin pour le fichier *aspnetcore-debug.log*, le fichier apparaît dans la liste.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-693">If you didn't supply a path for the *aspnetcore-debug.log* file, the file appears in the list.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-694">Si vous avez indiqué un chemin, accédez à l’emplacement du fichier journal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-694">If you supplied a path, navigate to the location of the log file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-696">Désactivez la journalisation du débogage, une fois la résolution des problèmes effectuée :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-696">Disable debug logging when troubleshooting is complete:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-697">Pour désactiver la journalisation de débogage améliorée, effectuez l’une des opérations suivantes :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-697">To disable the enhanced debug log, perform either of the following:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-699">Utilisez la console Kudu pour modifier le fichier *web.config* et supprimer la section `<handlerSettings>`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-699">Use the Kudu console to edit the *web.config* file and remove the `<handlerSettings>` section.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-700">Enregistrez le fichier .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-700">Save the file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="cab6e-701">Pour plus d’informations, consultez <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-701">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs>.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-702">Si le journal de débogage n’est pas désactivé, cela peut entraîner une défaillance de l’application ou du serveur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-702">Failure to disable the debug log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-703">Il n’existe aucune limite à la taille du fichier journal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-703">There's no limit on log file size.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cab6e-704">Utilisez uniquement la journalisation de débogage pour résoudre les problèmes de démarrage d’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-704">Only use debug logging to troubleshoot app startup problems.</span></span>

### <a name="slow-or-hanging-app-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="cab6e-707">Application lente ou suspendue (Azure App Service)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cab6e-707">Slow or hanging app (Azure App Service)</span></span>
